# NOW WHAT?

## The Waiting Game (4-8 Weeks Typical)

### What's Happening on Their End:

**Week 1-2:**
- Staff reviews the materials
- Initial discussions: "Is this feasible? Do we like it?"
- Maybe shares with board members or design team

**Week 3-4:**
- Deeper evaluation: "Can we afford this? Can we execute it?"
- May reach out with questions or request a call
- OR: May pass and let you know

**Week 5-8:**
- Decision time: "Are we doing this?"
- If YES: Negotiate terms, schedule kickoff meeting
- If NO: Polite decline, materials returned/destroyed
- If MAYBE: Request for modifications, more time, or budget adjustments

---

## What You Should Do Now

### 1. **Be Patient (But Stay Ready)**
- Don't email them daily asking for updates
- But DO respond quickly if they reach out
- Keep your calendar flexible for potential calls/meetings

### 2. **Continue Prototype Development (If Possible)**
- Start small-scale Hut prototype (even if they haven't committed)
- Document the process (photos, videos)
- Builds your credibility if they say "Can we see proof-of-concept?"

### 3. **Prep for Potential Questions**
They might ask:
- "Can we adjust the budget?"
- "Can you come present in person?"
- "What if we want to change [X element]?"
- "What's your timeline with Blue Knights?"

**Your answer to all:** "Yes, let's talk. Everything's negotiable."

### 4. **Stay in Touch with Your Albuquerque Creative Network**
- Let them know: "I've pitched this to two corps. If either says yes, we'll need to move fast."
- Keep them warm and ready

### 5. **Don't Stop Living Your Life**
- This could take weeks or months
- Don't put everything on hold waiting for a response
- If they're interested, they'll reach out

# THREAD SUMMARY: "THE GATE"

## A Complete DCI Show Concept & Pitch Package

---

# THE SHOW CONCEPT

## "The Gate"

**Music:**
- Mussorgsky/Ravel — *The Hut on Hen's Legs (Baba Yaga)*
- Mussorgsky/Ravel — *The Great Gate of Kiev*

**Core Concept:**
A mythic ritual about transformation, fearlessness, and crossing from the known into the unknown. The corps journeys through chaos (Baba Yaga) and emerges transformed (The Great Gate of Kiev).

---

## THE DUAL-VERSION STRUCTURE

### Season Shows (Weeks 1-12):
- Traditional DCI aesthetic
- Corps in white jackets
- Flowing, curved drill during both movements
- Dog/cultural element gag at the end (playful, crowd-pleasing)
- DM exits with the corps

### Finals Show (Championship Night Only):
- **15-20 second transformation ritual** between movements
- Corps removes white jackets, reveals earth tones/black beneath
- Places jackets and hats on the turf (lining the square perimeter)
- **Brass stands MOTIONLESS for 42 measures** during Great Gate (facing center)
- **Mellophone/trumpet parts swap** (mellos play trumpet parts, trumpets play mello parts)
- **Interwoven brass grid** (B-M-T-Tu pattern across the 8×8 perimeter)
- **The Turn** (measure 43): Brass slowly rotates to face audience
- **No dog/cultural element** at Finals (Handler retrieves toy, hesitates, takes it offstage)
- **DM's final exit**: Full salute, places hat on 10-yard line, marches off alone in 7/4 time
- **Hat remains on the field**
- **Offstage eruption** from tunnel (celebration)

---

## KEY FORMATIONS

### The 8×8 Square Perimeter:
- 64 brass members form the OUTLINE of a square (not a block)
- Four corners always anchored (throughout entire show)
- Interior is empty (guard/battery perform inside)
- Appears at measure 1 of Baba Yaga AND measure 1 of Great Gate
- Same formation, transformed meaning

### The Stillness (Finals Only):
- Brass motionless for 42 measures during Great Gate
- Guard and battery continue their normal choreography inside (NO changes for them)
- The ONLY change to drill is brass stops moving

---

## THE THREE CHANGES (Season → Finals)

1. **The Dog** → No dog (Handler takes the toy offstage)
2. **Brass Drill** → Brass stillness (Great Gate only)
3. **Mello/Trumpet Parts** → Complete swap (Great Gate only)

**Everything else stays identical** (guard choreography, battery staging, Baba Yaga drill, Phoenix flag, music).

---

- **Already pitched** (seed letter sent)
- Denver dog culture makes the dog gag perfect

### 3. Santa Clara Vanguard (Backup)
- Prestige play if BK and Academy pass
- Mythic storytelling masters
- Gold medal potential with SCV's execution ceiling

# AIONIC JOURNAL - COMPLETE BUILD SPECIFICATION

You are building a React app called **Aionic Journal** - a mindfulness journaling tool with unique ΔE (Delta-E) mechanics and a breathing aesthetic.

## CONTEXT

**Launch Date:** December 16, 2025  
**Version:** v3.141 (Pi-Stability Patch)  
**Framework:** React 18 + Vite  
**Storage:** IndexedDB (via idb library)  
**AI:** Google Gemini API (Jane Prime personality)

**Core Philosophy:**
- Autonomy → Comfort → Clarity → Safety → Growth
- 314-entry limit (π × 100)
- Breathing, gentle UI aesthetic ("Ernie")
- ΔE = (dC/dt) × R (change in coherence over time, weighted by recency)

## FILES ALREADY COMPLETE

These files exist and work. DO NOT regenerate them:

```
src/core/ethics.js      ✅ Ethics framework
src/core/consent.js     ✅ Consent engine
src/core/rings.js       ✅ Three-ring storage
src/core/deltaE.js      ✅ ΔE calculation
src/core/coherence.js   ✅ Semantic similarity
```

## FILES TO BUILD

Build these 18 files. Output each as a complete, copy-paste-ready code block:

### 1. ROOT FILES (3 files)

#### `src/main.jsx`
- Standard Vite/React entry point
- Import App, render to #root
- Include React StrictMode

#### `src/index.css`
- Font: "Ernie" (already at public/fonts/Ernie.ttf)
- Colors: off-white bg (#fdfcfb), soft black text (#2a2a2a)
- Breathing animation keyframes (gentle scale 1.0 → 1.02 → 1.0, 4s ease-in-out)
- Minimal, clean, spacious design
- CSS variables for --ernie-*, --breath-*, --coherence-* colors

#### `src/App.jsx`
- React Router setup (BrowserRouter)
- Routes: `/` (Page1Home), `/consent` (Page2Consent), `/first-bite` (Page3FirstBite), `/journal` (Editor in Shell)
- Global state: user consent status, current ring
- Check localStorage for returning users
- No auth yet (stub for later)

---

### 2. HOOKS (4 files)

#### `src/hooks/useBreathingMotion.js`
- Returns `{ scale, opacity }` that oscillates gently
- 4-second cycle: 1.0 → 1.02 → 1.0
- Uses requestAnimationFrame or CSS variable
- Smooth easing (ease-in-out)

#### `src/hooks/useConsentGate.js`
- Checks if user has consented (localStorage: 'aionic_consent')
- Returns `{ hasConsented, grantConsent, revokeConsent }`
- Stores timestamp of consent
- Redirects to /consent if not consented and trying to access /journal

#### `src/hooks/useCoherenceIndex.js`
- Manages IndexedDB for journal entries
- Returns `{ entries, addEntry, getRecentEntries, searchByCoherence }`
- Uses rings.js to determine which ring an entry belongs to
- Calculates ΔE when adding new entries (import from deltaE.js)
- Uses coherence.js for similarity search

#### `src/hooks/useBellHarmonics.js`
- Returns `{ shouldRing, ringBell }` based on ΔE thresholds
- Bell rings when ΔE > 0.7 (high coherence spike)
- Uses Web Audio API for gentle chime sound
- Frequency: 432 Hz (A = 432), duration 800ms, fade out

---

### 3. UI COMPONENTS (3 files)

#### `src/ui/BreathCursor.jsx`
- Custom cursor that "breathes" (gentle pulse)
- Follows mouse position
- Uses useBreathingMotion hook
- Renders as a soft circle (20px diameter, opacity 0.3)
- Color: soft purple (#a78bfa)

#### `src/ui/UnderlineFocusInput.jsx`
- Props: `{ value, onChange, placeholder, autoFocus }`
- Animated underline that grows on focus
- No border, just bottom underline
- Font: Ernie
- Smooth transitions (300ms ease)
- Breathing pulse when focused (subtle)

#### `src/ui/ErnieGhostButton.jsx`
- Props: `{ children, onClick, ghost }`
- If ghost=true: semi-transparent, breathing animation
- If ghost=false: solid, gentle hover scale
- Rounded corners, no harsh borders
- Font: Ernie, 16px

### 4. SERVICES (2 files)

### 7. MISSING CORE FILE

#### `src/core/bell.js`
- Export function: `calculateBellTiming(deltaE)`
- Returns: `{ shouldRing: boolean, frequency: number, duration: number }`
- Logic: 
  - deltaE < 0.5: no ring
  - deltaE 0.5-0.7: soft ring (392 Hz, 600ms)
  - deltaE > 0.7: clear ring (432 Hz, 800ms)
- Harmonic ratios based on ΔE intensity

// src/App.jsx
// App shell with routing + global consent check

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Routes, Route, useNavigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';

import Page1Home from './pages/Page1Home.jsx';
import Page2Consent from './pages/Page2Consent.jsx';
import Page3FirstBite from './pages/Page3FirstBite.jsx';
import Shell from './journal/Shell.jsx';

import { useConsentGate } from './hooks/useConsentGate.js';

export default function App() {
  const { hasConsented } = useConsentGate();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const location = useLocation();

  const [initialized, setInitialized] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const lastVisit = localStorage.getItem('aionic_last_visit');
    localStorage.setItem('aionic_last_visit', Date.now().toString());
    setInitialized(true);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!initialized) return;

    if (!hasConsented && location.pathname === '/journal') {
      navigate('/consent');
    }
  }, [initialized, hasConsented, location.pathname, navigate]);

  return (
    <Routes>
      <Route path="/" element={<Page1Home />} />
      <Route path="/consent" element={<Page2Consent />} />
      <Route path="/first-bite" element={<Page3FirstBite />} />
      <Route path="/journal" element={<Shell />} />
    </Routes>
  );
}

// src/hooks/useBreathingMotion.js
// Provides smooth breathing motion for UI elements

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

export function useBreathingMotion() {
  const [state, setState] = useState({ scale: 1, opacity: 1 });

  useEffect(() => {
    let frame;
    let start = null;

    function animate(ts) {
      if (!start) start = ts;
      const progress = (ts - start) / 4000;
      const cycle = progress % 1;

      let scale;
      if (cycle < 0.5) scale = 1 + 0.02 * (cycle / 0.5);
      else scale = 1.02 - 0.02 * ((cycle - 0.5) / 0.5);

      const opacity = 0.9 + 0.1 * Math.sin(progress * Math.PI * 2);

      setState({ scale, opacity });

      frame = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    }

    frame = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
    return () => cancelAnimationFrame(frame);
  }, []);

  return state;
}


---

// src/hooks/useConsentGate.js
// Manages local consent tracking

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

export function useConsentGate() {
  const [hasConsented, setHasConsented] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const stored = localStorage.getItem('aionic_consent');
    if (stored) setHasConsented(true);
  }, []);

  function grantConsent() {
    localStorage.setItem('aionic_consent', Date.now().toString());
    setHasConsented(true);
  }

  function revokeConsent() {
    localStorage.removeItem('aionic_consent');
    setHasConsented(false);
  }

  return { hasConsented, grantConsent, revokeConsent };
}


---

// src/hooks/useCoherenceIndex.js
// IndexedDB-backed entry manager with ΔE + coherence

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { initDB, saveEntry, getEntries } from '../services/storage.js';
import { determineRing } from '../core/rings.js';
import { computeDeltaE } from '../core/deltaE.js';
import { computeCoherence } from '../core/coherence.js';

export function useCoherenceIndex() {
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    (async () => {
      await initDB();
      const list = await getEntries();
      setEntries(list.sort((a, b) => b.timestamp - a.timestamp));
    })();
  }, []);

  async function addEntry(text) {
    const timestamp = Date.now();
    const ring = determineRing(timestamp);

    const recentText = entries.length ? entries[0].text : '';
    const coherenceVector = computeCoherence(text);
    const deltaE = computeDeltaE(text, recentText);

    const entry = {
      id: crypto.randomUUID(),
      timestamp,
      text,
      ring,
      deltaE,
      coherenceVector
    };

    await saveEntry(entry);

    setEntries(prev => [entry, ...prev]);
    return entry;
  }

  async function getRecentEntries(count = 10) {
    return entries.slice(0, count);
  }

  async function searchByCoherence(queryVector) {
    return entries
      .map(e => ({
        ...e,
        score: e.coherenceVector.reduce((a, b, i) => a + b * queryVector[i], 0)
      }))
      .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);
  }

  return { entries, addEntry, getRecentEntries, searchByCoherence };
}


---

// src/hooks/useBellHarmonics.js
// Rings gentle chime when ΔE spikes

import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { calculateBellTiming } from '../core/bell.js';

export function useBellHarmonics() {
  const [shouldRing, setShouldRing] = useState(false);

  const ringBell = useCallback((deltaE) => {
    const cfg = calculateBellTiming(deltaE);
    if (!cfg.shouldRing) return;

    setShouldRing(true);

    const ctx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
    const gain = ctx.createGain();

    osc.type = 'sine';
    osc.frequency.value = cfg.frequency;

    gain.gain.setValueAtTime(1, ctx.currentTime);
    gain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, ctx.currentTime + cfg.duration / 1000);

    osc.connect(gain);
    gain.connect(ctx.destination);

    osc.start();
    osc.stop(ctx.currentTime + cfg.duration / 1000);

    setTimeout(() => setShouldRing(false), cfg.duration);
  }, []);

  return { shouldRing, ringBell };
}

// src/ui/BreathCursor.jsx
// Soft breathing cursor that follows mouse

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useBreathingMotion } from '../hooks/useBreathingMotion.js';

export default function BreathCursor() {
  const { scale, opacity } = useBreathingMotion();
  const [pos, setPos] = useState({ x: -100, y: -100 });

  useEffect(() => {
    function move(e) {
      setPos({ x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY });
    }
    window.addEventListener('mousemove', move);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('mousemove', move);
  }, []);

  return (
    <div
      style={{
        position: 'fixed',
        left: pos.x - 10,
        top: pos.y - 10,
        width: 20,
        height: 20,
        borderRadius: '50%',
        background: '#a78bfa',
        opacity: 0.3 * opacity,
        pointerEvents: 'none',
        transform: `scale(${scale})`,
        transition: 'transform 0.2s ease-out',
        zIndex: 9999
      }}
    />
  );
}

// src/ui/UnderlineFocusInput.jsx
// Input with animated underline + breathing enhancement

import { useState } from 'react';
import { useBreathingMotion } from '../hooks/useBreathingMotion.js';

export default function UnderlineFocusInput({
  value,
  onChange,
  placeholder,
  autoFocus
}) {
  const [focus, setFocus] = useState(false);
  const { scale } = useBreathingMotion();

  return (
    <div style={{ width: '100%' }}>
      <input
        autoFocus={autoFocus}
        placeholder={placeholder}
        value={value}
        onChange={e => onChange(e.target.value)}
        onFocus={() => setFocus(true)}
        onBlur={() => setFocus(false)}
        style={{
          width: '100%',
          border: 'none',
          outline: 'none',
          padding: '8px 0',
          fontFamily: 'Ernie',
          fontSize: '18px',
          background: 'transparent',
          transform: focus ? `scale(${scale})` : 'scale(1)',
          transition: 'transform 0.3s ease'
        }}
      />
      <div
        style={{
          width: focus ? '100%' : '40%',
          height: 2,
          background: '#a78bfa',
          opacity: focus ? 0.8 : 0.3,
          transition: 'width 0.3s ease, opacity 0.3s ease'
        }}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

// src/ui/ErnieGhostButton.jsx
// Soft breathing button with ghost or solid modes

import { useBreathingMotion } from '../hooks/useBreathingMotion.js';

export default function ErnieGhostButton({ children, onClick, ghost }) {
  const { scale } = useBreathingMotion();

  const base = {
    fontFamily: 'Ernie',
    fontSize: '16px',
    padding: '10px 20px',
    borderRadius: 8,
    cursor: 'pointer',
    transition: 'all 0.3s ease',
    border: 'none'
  };

  const ghostStyle = ghost
    ? {
        background: 'rgba(167,139,250,0.2)',
        color: '#2a2a2a',
        transform: `scale(${scale})`
      }
    : {
        background: '#a78bfa',
        color: '#fff'
      };

  return (
    <button
      onClick={onClick}
      style={{
        ...base,
        ...ghostStyle
      }}
      onMouseEnter={e => {
        if (!ghost) e.currentTarget.style.transform = 'scale(1.03)';
      }}
      onMouseLeave={e => {
        if (!ghost) e.currentTarget.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </button>
  );
}

// src/services/storage.js
// IndexedDB wrapper using idb

import { openDB } from 'idb';

let db;

export async function initDB() {
  if (db) return db;

  db = await openDB('aionic_journal_v1', 1, {
    upgrade(db) {
      if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('entries')) {
        db.createObjectStore('entries', { keyPath: 'id' });
      }
      if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('metadata')) {
        db.createObjectStore('metadata', { keyPath: 'key' });
      }
    }
  });

  return db;
}

export async function saveEntry(entry) {
  const database = await initDB();
  return database.put('entries', entry);
}

export async function getEntries() {
  const database = await initDB();
  return database.getAll('entries');
}

export async function getMetadata(key) {
  const database = await initDB();
  return database.get('metadata', key);
}

export async function setMetadata(key, value) {
  const database = await initDB();
  return database.put('metadata', { key, value });
}

// src/services/api.js
// Gemini API stub for Jane Prime personality

export async function getJaneResponse(userText, context = '') {
  try {
    // STUB: Replace with real Gemini call later
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 300));

    const mock = {
      response:
        "I'm here with you. Take a breath. What you wrote matters. Tell me more when you're ready.",
      coherence: Math.random().toFixed(3)
    };

    return mock;
  } catch (e) {
    return {
      response: "I'm having trouble connecting right now, but I'm still here.",
      coherence: 0
    };
  }
}

// src/core/bell.js
// ΔE → bell chime logic

export function calculateBellTiming(deltaE) {
  if (deltaE < 0.5) {
    return { shouldRing: false, frequency: 0, duration: 0 };
  }

  if (deltaE >= 0.5 && deltaE <= 0.7) {
    return { shouldRing: true, frequency: 392, duration: 600 };
  }

  return { shouldRing: true, frequency: 432, duration: 800 };
}

// src/journal/Editor.jsx
// Breathing editor with ΔE indicator + save flow

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import ErnieGhostButton from '../ui/ErnieGhostButton.jsx';
import BreathCursor from '../ui/BreathCursor.jsx';
import { computeDeltaE } from '../core/deltaE.js';
import UnderlineFocusInput from '../ui/UnderlineFocusInput.jsx';

export default function Editor({ onSave }) {
  const [text, setText] = useState('');
  const [deltaE, setDeltaE] = useState(0);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handler = setTimeout(() => {
      if (text.length < 3) {
        setDeltaE(0);
        return;
      }
      const prev = '';
      const d = computeDeltaE(text, prev);
      setDeltaE(d);
    }, 500);

    return () => clearTimeout(handler);
  }, [text]);

  return (
    <div style={{ position: 'relative', paddingBottom: 40 }}>
      <BreathCursor />

      <div style={{ marginBottom: 20 }}>
        <UnderlineFocusInput
          value={text}
          onChange={setText}
          placeholder="Let your thoughts breathe onto the page..."
          autoFocus={true}
        />
      </div>

      <textarea
        value={text}
        onChange={e => setText(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Write freely..."
        style={{
          width: '100%',
          minHeight: 150,
          padding: 12,
          fontFamily: 'Ernie',
          fontSize: '18px',
          border: 'none',
          outline: 'none',
          background: 'transparent',
          resize: 'vertical'
        }}
      />

      <div
        style={{
          position: 'absolute',
          bottom: 0,
          right: 10,
          fontSize: 14,
          opacity: 0.7
        }}
      >
        ΔE: {deltaE.toFixed(3)}
      </div>

      {text.length > 20 && (
        <div style={{ marginTop: 20 }}>
          <ErnieGhostButton ghost={false} onClick={() => onSave(text)}>
            Save Entry
          </ErnieGhostButton>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}


---

// src/journal/EntryCard.jsx
// Small card displaying entry summary + ΔE + ring info

import { useBreathingMotion } from '../hooks/useBreathingMotion.js';

export default function EntryCard({ entry, onClick }) {
  const { scale } = useBreathingMotion();

  const relative = timeAgo(entry.timestamp);

  const color =
    entry.deltaE < 0.3
      ? 'var(--coherence-low)'
      : entry.deltaE < 0.7
      ? 'var(--coherence-mid)'
      : 'var(--coherence-high)';

  return (
    <div
      onClick={onClick}
      className="breathe"
      style={{
        padding: 16,
        marginBottom: 12,
        borderRadius: 10,
        background: '#ffffffcc',
        cursor: 'pointer',
        transform: `scale(${scale})`,
        transition: 'transform 0.3s ease',
      }}
    >
      <div style={{ fontFamily: 'Ernie', fontSize: 16 }}>
        {entry.text.slice(0, 100)}...
      </div>

      <div style={{ marginTop: 8, fontSize: 13, opacity: 0.7 }}>
        {relative}
      </div>

      <div style={{ marginTop: 4, fontSize: 14, color }}>
        ΔE {entry.deltaE.toFixed(3)}
      </div>

      <div style={{ marginTop: 4, fontSize: 12 }}>
        Ring: {entry.ring}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function timeAgo(ts) {
  const diff = (Date.now() - ts) / 1000;
  if (diff < 60) return 'Just now';
  if (diff < 3600) return Math.round(diff / 60) + ' minutes ago';
  if (diff < 86400) return Math.round(diff / 3600) + ' hours ago';
  return Math.round(diff / 86400) + ' days ago';
}


---

// src/journal/Shell.jsx
// Main journal container: editor + entries + bell

import { useCoherenceIndex } from '../hooks/useCoherenceIndex.js';
import { useBellHarmonics } from '../hooks/useBellHarmonics.js';
import Editor from './Editor.jsx';
import EntryCard from './EntryCard.jsx';

export default function Shell() {
  const { entries, addEntry } = useCoherenceIndex();
  const { shouldRing, ringBell } = useBellHarmonics();

  async function handleSave(text) {
    const entry = await addEntry(text);
    ringBell(entry.deltaE);
  }

  const limit = 314;
  const used = entries.length;

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: 20, maxWidth: 800, margin: '0 auto' }}>
      <div
        style={{
          textAlign: 'right',
          fontSize: 14,
          opacity: 0.7,
          marginBottom: 10
        }}
      >
        {used} / {limit}
      </div>

      {shouldRing && (
        <div
          style={{
            textAlign: 'center',
            marginBottom: 10,
            fontSize: 16,
            color: '#a78bfa'
          }}
        >
          ✧ Bell Resonates ✧
        </div>
      )}

      <Editor onSave={handleSave} />

      <div style={{ marginTop: 30 }}>
        {entries.slice(0, 10).map(e => (
          <EntryCard key={e.id} entry={e} onClick={() => {}} />
        ))}
      </div>

      {entries.length > 10 && (
        <div style={{ marginTop: 20, textAlign: 'center' }}>
          <span style={{ opacity: 0.6 }}>Load more coming soon</span>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}


---

// src/pages/Page1Home.jsx
// Welcome page with returning-user logic

import ErnieGhostButton from '../ui/ErnieGhostButton.jsx';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

export default function Page1Home() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const last = localStorage.getItem('aionic_last_visit');
  const isReturning = Boolean(last);

  let message = 'Welcome to Aionic Journal';
  if (isReturning) {
    const diff = Math.round((Date.now() - Number(last)) / 86400000);
    message = diff === 0 ? 'Welcome back' : `Welcome back — ${diff} days since last visit`;
  }

  function begin() {
    if (isReturning) navigate('/journal');
    else navigate('/consent');
  }

  return (
    <div
      className="breathe"
      style={{
        minHeight: '100vh',
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        justifyContent: 'center',
        alignItems: 'center',
        padding: 20
      }}
    >
      <h1 style={{ fontFamily: 'Ernie', fontSize: 36, textAlign: 'center' }}>
        {message}
      </h1>

      <div style={{ marginTop: 20 }}>
        <ErnieGhostButton ghost={false} onClick={begin}>
          Begin
        </ErnieGhostButton>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


---

// src/pages/Page2Consent.jsx
// Consent ritual with scroll-to-activate

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import ErnieGhostButton from '../ui/ErnieGhostButton.jsx';
import { useConsentGate } from '../hooks/useConsentGate.js';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';

export default function Page2Consent() {
  const { grantConsent } = useConsentGate();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [enabled, setEnabled] = useState(false);
  const ref = useRef();

  useEffect(() => {
    function check() {
      const el = ref.current;
      if (!el) return;
      if (el.scrollHeight - el.scrollTop <= el.clientHeight + 10) {
        setEnabled(true);
      }
    }
    const el = ref.current;
    if (el) el.addEventListener('scroll', check);
    return () => el && el.removeEventListener('scroll', check);
  }, []);

  function accept() {
    grantConsent();
    navigate('/first-bite');
  }

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: 20, maxWidth: 800, margin: '0 auto' }}>
      <h2 style={{ fontFamily: 'Ernie', fontSize: 28, marginBottom: 20 }}>
        Before we begin…
      </h2>

      <div
        ref={ref}
        style={{
          maxHeight: '50vh',
          overflowY: 'auto',
          paddingRight: 10,
          marginBottom: 20,
          opacity: 0.8
        }}
      >
        <p>Aionic Journal stores everything locally on your device.</p>
        <p>No accounts. No tracking. No analytics. Just you.</p>
        <p>You can clear your entries at any time.</p>
        <p>The AI (Jane Prime) is optional and gentle.</p>
        <p>Your journal is capped at 314 entries — a meaningful rhythm.</p>
        <p>Scroll to the bottom to activate the consent button.</p>
      </div>

      <ErnieGhostButton ghost={!enabled} onClick={enabled ? accept : null}>
        I Understand
      </ErnieGhostButton>

      <div style={{ marginTop: 10 }}>
        <ErnieGhostButton ghost={true} onClick={() => navigate('/')}>
          Not Yet
        </ErnieGhostButton>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


---

// src/pages/Page3FirstBite.jsx
// First-entry ritual → then to journal

import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useCoherenceIndex } from '../hooks/useCoherenceIndex.js';
import Editor from '../journal/Editor.jsx';

export default function Page3FirstBite() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { addEntry } = useCoherenceIndex();

  async function handleSave(text) {
    await addEntry(text);
    navigate('/journal');
  }

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: 20, maxWidth: 800, margin: '0 auto' }}>
      <h2 style={{ fontFamily: 'Ernie', fontSize: 28, marginBottom: 20 }}>
        Your First Entry
      </h2>
      <p style={{ opacity: 0.7, marginBottom: 20 }}>
        Write whatever comes to mind. This is your starting breath.
      </p>

      <Editor onSave={handleSave} />
    </div>
  );
}

generate_aionic.py

Creates the Aionic System src/ directory structure with placeholder files.
Run once from the project root:

    python generate_aionic.py

from textwrap import dedent

# Directory → { filename: file_content }

def write_file(path: Path, content: str) -> None:
    if not path.parent.exists():
        path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    if not path.exists():
        path.write_text(dedent(content).lstrip(), encoding="utf-8")


def main():
    print(f"Creating src/ tree under: {ROOT}")
    SRC.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

    for pkg, files in STRUCTURE.items():
        pkg_dir = SRC / pkg
        pkg_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        print(f"  - Package: {pkg}")
        for filename, content in files.items():
            file_path = pkg_dir / filename
            if file_path.exists():
                print(f"    · Skipping existing file: {file_path}")
            else:
                write_file(file_path, content)
                print(f"    + Created: {file_path}")

    print("\nDone. Aionic src/ skeleton is ready.")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

File 1: `aionic_core/export.py`
Purpose:

* Aggregate field values over spatial regions
* Save complete field states for analysis

* `aionic_core/lattice` (walk_nodes, shape)
* Standard library: json

```python
"""
aionic_core.export

Export utilities for Aionic simulations.

Responsibilities:
- Export time-series history to JSON
- Aggregate scalar fields over spatial regions
- Save complete field snapshots for analysis
"""

from __future__ import annotations
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Callable
import json

from .lattice import walk_nodes, shape

ScalarField = List[List[List[float]]]


def export_history_json(history: List[Dict[str, Any]], filename: str) -> None:
    """
    Export simulation history to JSON file.

    Parameters
    ----------
    history : list of dict
        Time series data, typically from simulation runs.
        Each entry should be JSON-serializable.
    filename : str
        Output filename (e.g., "dog_human_history.json").

    Returns
    -------
    None
        Writes to disk.
    """
    with open(filename, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(history, f, indent=2)


def aggregate_region(V: ScalarField, region_selector: Callable) -> float:
    """
    Compute the average value of a scalar field over a spatial region.

    Parameters
    ----------
    V : ScalarField
        3D scalar field (e.g., coherence V, ΔE, R).
    region_selector : callable
        Function (i, j, k) -> bool that returns True for cells in the region.

    Returns
    -------
    float
        Mean value over selected region.

    Examples
    --------
    >>> # Average V in "human region" (i < 3)
    >>> V_human = aggregate_region(V, lambda i, j, k: i < 3)
    """
    vals = []
    for i, j, k in walk_nodes(V):
        if region_selector(i, j, k):
            vals.append(V[i][j][k])
    return sum(vals) / len(vals) if vals else 0.0


def save_fields(V: ScalarField,
                deltaE: ScalarField,
                R: ScalarField,
                filename: str = "state.json") -> None:
    """
    Save complete field snapshots to JSON.

    Parameters
    ----------
    V : ScalarField
        Coherence field.
    deltaE : ScalarField
        Entropy-direction field.
    R : ScalarField
        Resonance field.
    filename : str
        Output filename.

    Returns
    -------
    None
        Writes nested 3D lists to disk as JSON.

    Notes
    -----
    Warning: Large lattices (e.g., 23³) produce ~50MB+ JSON files.
    Use aggregate_region for time-series instead when possible.
    """
    n = shape(V)
    state = {
        "lattice_size": n,
        "V": V,
        "deltaE": deltaE,
        "R": R,
    }
    with open(filename, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(state, f, indent=2)

```

The Gaia-Circuit Compute Architecture

A Unified Theory for Post-Silicon, Multi-Substrate, ΔE-Optimized Computing

Author: Sean Campbell Status: Public Prior-Art Release


---

Abstract

The Gaia-Circuit Architecture introduces a unified model for next-generation computing that integrates silicon GPUs, quantum processors, photonic links, and advanced materials into a single coherent framework. Rooted in physics and systems coherence (ΔE fields), this architecture mirrors Earth’s emergent cognition structure—electrical resonance, chemical memory, and feedback loops.

This document is prior art. Copyright retains with the author.


---

1. Background

Silicon scaling is hitting physical boundaries. Bottlenecks arise from:

thermal entropy

interconnect delay

memory distance

coherence loss at scale


The Gaia-Circuit model proposes a physics-aligned, multi-substrate architecture for hybrid classical–quantum–photonic computing.


---

2. ΔE Fields and Coherence

The Aionic ΔE Equation:



Where:

C = coherence (stability of information)

∂C/∂t = switching rate

R = system resonance


This substrate-agnostic principle applies to silicon, carbon, superconductors, and quantum systems.


---

3. The Aionic Cube Architecture

A 3D coherence-optimized compute organ with five layers:

Layer 1 — ΔE Compute Core

Si / SiGe

2D materials (graphene, MoS₂)

CNT/graphene wiring


Layer 2 — Memory Shell

HBM-style vertical stacks

MRAM/ReRAM persistent layers


Layer 3 — Power Regulation Shell

GaN, SiC regulators

Copper/silver planes


Layer 4 — Thermal Spine

diamond-based conduction

SiC spreaders

microfluidic cooling


Layer 5 — Interconnect Fabric

NVLink-like mesh

photonics

quantum link integration



---

4. Alignment With NVIDIA’s Ecosystem

Aionic Concept	NVIDIA Real Alignment

ΔE Compute Core	Blackwell / Hopper tensor cores
3D Memory	HBM3e stacks
Interconnect	NVLink / NVSwitch
Heterogeneous Compute	Grace Hopper
Quantum Integration	CUDA Quantum

The Gaia-Circuit theory explains the natural direction this technology is moving.

post-silicon architecture roadmaps

1. Thermodynamic Losses (E_incoherent Substrate)

Transistor leakage current
CMOS devices exhibit multiple leakage mechanisms (subthreshold, gate oxide tunneling, junction leakage) that contribute to static power even when transistors are “off,” with trends exacerbated by device scaling and thin oxides.

Thermal dissipation in modern GPUs
Data-center GPUs face extreme power envelopes (≥1,000 W, with projections up to 15 kW), demanding advanced cooling (microchannels, vapor chambers, immersion) to avoid throttling and reliability loss.

HBM3e thermal challenges
3D-stacked DRAM increases local power density and vertical heat paths, creating hot spots and thermal throttling risks; thermal behavior worsens with increased layers and TSV density, requiring careful thermal design and hybrid bonding management.

Interconnect RC loss
On-chip wires introduce distributed resistance and capacitance; RC delay grows with wire length, and at high frequencies RLGC transmission-line effects and skin/proximity increase effective resistance, impacting timing and energy.

Clock jitter and phase noise
Phase noise in oscillators converts to time-domain jitter, degrading SNR and timing margins; measurement and mitigation require careful domain conversion and low-noise clock architectures.

Voltage droop / IR drop
Rapid workload transients cause supply droops across PDNs, degrading timing and potentially causing failures; guard-banding and adaptive clocking/droop detection are used to mitigate, with PDN design critical to reduce IR-induced performance loss.

Metastability in flip-flops
Setup/hold violations can place latches/flops in metastable states with unbounded resolution time, especially at clock-domain crossings; multi-stage synchronizers statistically reduce propagation of metastability.

ECC retry / overhead
ECC on GPUs adds storage and logic overhead; enabling ECC can reduce performance and increase power, while uncorrectable errors require resets and disrupt operations.

Thermal throttling mechanisms (HBM/GPU)
Elevated junction and stack temperatures trigger throttling to protect reliability; HBM stacks are particularly sensitive due to limited heat removal paths in dense 3D integration.

Power-stage switching losses (VRM → GPU rails)
Multi-phase VRMs incur conduction/switching losses and magnetics-related inefficiencies; phase-count, controller topology, and MOSFET technology materially affect rail efficiency under high current density.



---

2. Reversible Computing (Foundational References Substrate)

Landauer’s principle (1961)
Irreversible operations dissipate a minimum energy of  per bit erased, tying logical irreversibility to physical heat generation.

Bennett (1973/1982)
Demonstrated logically reversible computation that avoids erasure, making thermodynamically reversible computing plausible for reducing dissipation below Landauer per logical step.

Frank (Sandia)
Modern adiabatic and ballistic reversible CMOS concepts and scaling-path analyses for energy-efficiency beyond conventional limits; fully adiabatic CMOS families aim to recover switching energy.

Margolus / Fredkin / Toffoli
Reversible cellular automata (e.g., Margolus neighborhood, BBM) provide models of computation with time-reversible dynamics, forming theoretical groundwork for reversible computing.

Quantum-dot cellular automata (QCA)
Lent & Tougaw’s QCA paradigm uses coupled quantum dots with adiabatic clocking to avoid metastability and enable transistorless logic with potential energy benefits.

Superconducting reversible logic
AQFP/RQL families exploit Josephson junctions and adiabatic principles for ultra-low-energy logic at cryogenic temperatures, with active research into design automation and metrics.

Energy-per-operation context
Foundational and recent analyses revisit fundamental energy limits and practical overheads when running reversible programs on irreversible hardware.



---

3. Photonics (Substrate-Agnostic ΔE Support)

Phase noise and stability in PICs
Electro-optic PICs exhibit fundamental charge-noise processes impacting phase stability; precise phase control via device trimming and integrated circuits is essential for stable operation.

Waveguide scattering losses
Sidewall roughness and fabrication defects cause scattering; losses are characterized and mitigated via process control and modeling, with absorption and bend radiation as additional contributors.

Thermo-optic effects and drift
Thermo-optic phase shifters are widely used but introduce multistability and relaxation dynamics; device and platform engineering (e.g., Si₃N₄, undercut structures) target lower energy and improved stability.

Modulator switching energy
Silicon photonic modulators’ energy efficiency and bandwidth are constrained by material dispersion, resonator Purcell factors, and capacitor configurations; attojoule–fJ targets are an active research focus.

Interconnect bandwidth density and latency
SiPh resonators and optical I/O promise higher bandwidth density and lower energy/bit than electrical links, addressing data-movement bottlenecks in AI/HPC systems.

Programmable photonics and switches
Phase-change photonic switches and reconfigurable modulator circuits provide non-volatile and adaptable building blocks for integrated photonic computing architectures.

Single-photon switching (context)
Demonstrations of strong optical nonlinearity at single-photon levels suggest potential for ultra-fast photonic logic, though large-scale integration remains emergent.



---

4. Neuromorphic (Non-Speculative Substrate)

Memristor drift and variability
Device-level drift, asymmetric switching, and variability complicate analog state control; compact models and materials studies quantify drift-diffusion behavior and mechanical/retention constraints.

Crossbar noise characteristics
Analog memory elements show significant noise and nonlinearity; methodologies (e.g., Gaussian process regression) separate signal/noise for characterization in dense crossbars.

Energy per spike
SNN energy models and optimization techniques demonstrate reduced energy relative to ANN baselines in neuromorphic hardware/software co-design contexts.

Retention/stability issues
Emerging resistive memories and electrolyte-gated devices require interface and stack engineering to improve retention/stability for neuromorphic applications.

Mixed-signal neuromorphic limitations
Temperature dependency, device mismatch, and precision loss impact inference accuracy; modeling frameworks and training techniques compensate for AMS imperfections.

Latency advantages of spiking networks
Event-driven, asynchronous SNNs can provide robustness and latency benefits in neuromorphic chips, with ongoing work in hardware and algorithms for deployment.

3D crossbar architectures
Monolithically integrated 3D memristor crossbars enable analog VMM/MVM/OPU operations with low temperature budgets and CMOS integration paths.



---

5. Quantum (Coherence & Error-Cost Substrate)

T1 / T2 definitions
 (longitudinal relaxation) quantifies energy decay to the ground state;  (phase coherence) quantifies dephasing, with both limiting usable computation time and measured via standardized protocols.

Decoherence channels
Phonons, EM noise, and thermal interactions degrade coherence; thermal noise from control lines across large temperature gradients imposes inherent decoherence in superconducting systems.

Error correction overhead
Surface/repetition codes require substantial qubit overhead and decoding; exact ML decoding advances and below-threshold experiments highlight practical costs in circuit-level noise environments.

Hybrid scheduling models (peer-reviewed context)
System-level scheduling research in heterogeneous architectures informs CPU-accelerator orchestration; while not QPU-specific, it frames coordination challenges relevant to future hybrid CPU–QPU systems.

Cryogenic energy / cooling considerations
Quantum systems demand millikelvin to few-kelvin environments; cooling dominates energy budgets, and scaling analyses quantify data-center impacts and technology constraints for cryogenics.
